                        $('#filter_exclude').on('change', function() {
                            var checked = $(this).is(":checked");
                            if ( checked ) {
                                location.href = '/browse/games/score/metascore/allpc/all/all?sort=desc&page=0';
                            }
                            else {
                                location.href = '/browse/games/score/metascore/allpc/all/filtered?sort=desc&page=0';
